+    applyTemplate(title, type, km, days, desc) {
+      const form = this.$refs.reminderForm;
+      if (!form) return;
+      form.querySelector('[name=title]').value = title;
+      form.querySelector('[name=trigger_type]').value = type;
+      form.querySelector('[name=trigger_value_km]').value = km || '';
+      form.querySelector('[name=trigger_value_days]').value = days || '';
+      form.querySelector('[name=description]').value = desc;
+      form.querySelector('[name=is_recurring]').checked = true;
+      this.updateCompletion();
+    },
+
     showTip(field) {
       this.tips[field] = true;
     },
